    SELECT TOP(@__p_0) [g].[Id], [g].[CreateTime], [g].[CreatedByUserId], [g].[GuessedWord], [g].[LastGameUsageTime], [g].[RelatedWord], [g].[UpdateTime]
    FROM [GuessData] AS [g]
    ORDER BY [g].[LastGameUsageTime]
) AS [t]
ORDER BY [t].[LastGameUsageTime] DESC
